122→enum CSPKeyword {\n   123→#define KEYWORD_ENUM(id_, string_) id_,\n   124→  FOR_EACH_CSP_KEYWORD(KEYWORD_ENUM)\n   125→#undef KEYWORD_ENUM\n   126→\n   127→  // CSP_LAST_KEYWORD_VALUE always needs It implements the static method parseContentSecurityPolicy() which tokenizes and parses CSP policy strings according to the W3C CSP specification. The parser is a state machine that processes directives and source lists.\\n\\n**CSP Context and Policy Management:**\\nThe nsCSPContext class (dom/security/nsCSPContext.h/.cpp) implements the main CSP context that holds multiple policies and handles CSP enforcement.
